  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ

  dG_a = fun ρ =>

  fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b -

  ∀ (ρ : Idx),
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +

    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * Γtot M r θ ρ μ a)

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

  sumIdx B_b - Cμa + Cνa =
    sumIdx fun ρ => B_b ρ - Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b + Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b

  ((sumIdx B_b - sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b) +
      sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b) =
    -sumIdx fun ρ => RiemannUp M r θ ρ a μ ν * g M ρ b r θ

    0
